<Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
I just finished moving out of my apartment at OceanAire after living there for 9 months. I was moving to the Bay Area and needed to find something quick, easy, and safe and OceanAire was just that. I knew I couldn't stay long term due to it being out of my budget but it would be manageable for the short term with money I had saved. If money wasn't an issue I would have never left! They're pricey but it's definitely worth it.

Not only is the quality of living very high but their team of staff is what makes them truly stand out. Gina helped me from the beginning, showing me the units that were available and everything else after with getting approved and signing the lease. She should be the standard for leasing agents, so patient, warm and personable, and not pushy whatsoever.

The manager, Zee is also one of the nicest people I've come across in the CA rental industry. She's incredibly responsive to emails and any issues and is really everything you'd want in an apartment manager.

Maintenance requests were always resolved very quickly which was really nice. I really can't think of 1 bad or negative thing over the last 9 months I spent there. Definitely an amazing place to live if you have the chance, take it!</Review>

I really enjoyed my stay at OceanAire. The places are very well kept, as are the grounds. All my neighbors were really friendly. I enjoy having the car garage as well. Zee was the person I enjoyed working with most. She is a really genuine, sweet, and helpful person. I always enjoyed visiting with her, and she was very prompt and professional in all my dealings.

I would highly recommend OceanAire! Please tell Zee that Phil says hello if this review prompted you to contact OceanAire. She will be sure to take care of you.

Me and my friends were looking for a new one bedroom apartment close to San Francisco. We explored around 15 apartment complexes in South San Francisco. We set our priority according following criterias - location, price and conditions. Oceanarie Apartments is the one which met our expectations. It's located just by Pacific Ocean and 15 mins away from SF. Townhouses are renovated newly both exterior and interior. Also, we got $2000 off for signing lease agreement as a promotion. Now we are living here for last 6 months, and thinking to resign our lease for another 9 months. Special thanks to Veronica Avelar and Marisol Espino from leasing office. They are helpful. Also, beach access was restored, so now we have a full access to the beach</review>

['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPG0bUdF6Q0EeOCr4xnmc5xNo1N0bO-uCnVdEu7=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOzTh6ozB1unUN3SV8iiQX2HGVF7O11yANMqFyB=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNdED7cOxulvUo4BulQRTVtMfNQNDiRonWG6CJy=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pics><Date>1505606636195</Date><Review>Horrible Construction/Renovtion Disaster!!

I moved in 4 months ago and this has been going on for 3 months. It's 6 days a week of noise and 7 days a week of inconvenience, unsightly equipment, multiple dumpsters, materials, trash, construction vehicles and debris. My parking is in the other half of the complex, across the street, so I've been dealing with the mess since the beginning of the demo in June.

For over a month, the gym was closed, the common "oceanview patio with free wifi" was covered in junk, the common rec room was closed, and even the office was closed. They haven't used their app even once to broadcast messages to tenants. The grounds have been a disaster since mid-June -- as if they're not even going to pretend to keep up appearances.

In July, I stopped going down to look at the ocean, because they were ripping apart the buildings facing the ocean and it was just too depressing to see the mess everywhere. (PS - they said they were going to restore beach access that was washed out earlier in the year, but I'm not holding my breath. Google Maps still shows the path, but it's gone. Also the Oceanaire property map shows an ocean path, which is not there.)

They haven't done anything to contain the  work to a particular section of the property and complete one building before beginning demo on an adjacent building. Instead they work on another building on the opposite end. They are randomly criss-crossing lengthwise across the property (south-north) instead of working east-west). The way they're doing it, it's as if they're purposely trying to MAXIMIZE the  inconvenience of everyone and make it so that nothing looks pretty or peaceful or at all like home.

I was only given 6 days notice on 9/1 to clear my patio before 9/8 and to keep my windows closed for 2 months for renovation to my building. I had purchased $300 of patio furniture and plants when I moved here, not knowing that they were planning a major renovation and everything would all have to be stored inside.  4 days into my apartment renovation, the wrecking crew cut an electrical line to my kitchen and my refrigerator was without power for about 30 hours (and I'll have to toss everything). In the response to my online Maintenance request early that evening 9/12, a technician showed up at my door at 11:45 pm(!) and left at 12:45 am(!) without any resolution. The 2nd day they brought an extension cord. The 3rd day an electrician came to repair it and left the fridge hooked up to the extension cord and left a mess. The 4th day they came back to plug the fridge in properly and remove the extension cord (because I complained) and they still left the mess on the countertop, plus white handprints on my black fridge and countertop. < text>
I've been at OceanAire longer than most; four years in November. Over the years the community has had its ups & downs - most noticeably when it underwent major construction for about a year (which drove many of the negative reviews online). They've made some great positive changes since then, most notably in management of the community. This remains a really nice place to live - quiet, comfortable, and with an ideal location right on the ocean. The staff are terrific. They are highly responsive and the maintenance team is the best (particular shoutouts to Mike, Zee, and Omar).
With that said, lately I've been disappointed with the amenities that OceanAire promotes front & center on their website as a value-add to residents. That lovely spa that you see on the home page? Hasn't worked for months; basically all summer. The fitness center? Machines are frequently broken or not properly maintained, and bizarrely there is a personal trainer running her business out of it all day which monopolizes the equipment. Be careful investing too much value in the beach access, because this part of the coastline experiences major erosion, which means restoration efforts need to happen which block or disrupt that access. (The access was closed for over a year when a sinkhole took out a chunk of the path, and as of the time of writing this review the beach is a major construction site due to a necessary rebuild of the seawall.)
Overall, I still recommend OceanAire to prospective tenants, but please make your decision based solely on the apartment itself, and not in the peripheral amenities which have become unreliable and consequently far less valuable.</text>

< Text>
I've been at OceanAire longer than most; four years in November. Over the years the community has had its ups & downs - most noticeably when it underwent major construction for about a year (which drove many of the negative reviews online). They've made some great positive changes since then, most notably in management of the community. This remains a really nice place to live - quiet, comfortable, and with an ideal location right on the ocean. The staff are terrific. They are highly responsive and the maintenance team is the best (particular shoutouts to Mike, Zee, and Omar).
With that said, lately I've been disappointed with the amenities that OceanAire promotes front & center on their website as a value-add to residents. That lovely spa that you see on the home page? Hasn't worked for months; basically all summer. The fitness center? Machines are frequently broken or not properly maintained, and bizarrely there is a personal trainer running her business out of it all day which monopolizes the equipment. Be careful investing too much value in the beach access, because this part of the coastline experiences major erosion, which means restoration efforts need to happen which block or disrupt that access. (The access was closed for over a year when a sinkhole took out a chunk of the path, and as of the time of writing this review the beach is a major construction site due to a necessary rebuild of the seawall.)
Overall, I still recommend OceanAire to prospective tenants, but please make your decision based solely on the apartment itself, and not in the peripheral amenities which have become unreliable and consequently far less valuable.</Text>

<Text>Lands End is an amazing place to live!  We lived there for about 9 months and had to move for a job out of state.  The view is unbelievable and nearly all year round you can see whales, dolphins, sea lions, pelicans & more right from your apartment!  The only issues we had were that the garbage disposal broke, the fridge was shutting off and on & the dryer wasn't drying very well, but they resolved all of the issues quickly.  Some reviews complained about the washer/dryer combination machine not drying well, but the filter has to be cleaned every few months, so simply put in a work order and the dryer will work great after being cleaned.  The complex itself is a little older and we can often hear our neighbors upstairs, but we would definitely continue to live here if we were staying in Pacifica.  It is clean, safe and very peaceful.  It is very close to Safeway, good restaurants and Hwy 1.  It was also nice to have a gym, jacuzzi & clubhouse that I could walk to in less than a minute.  The price for the SF Bay Area is reasonable; you will pay about what you'd pay in many other apt. complexes in the area but this one is right on the ocean!  But nothing's perfect...you will not get all of your security deposit back; you will have to pay for carpet shampooing, repainting, apartment cleaning, etc. when you move out.< /Text>< time>

<Rating>5</Rating>< Review>
Bill Kennedys shop  is a "mom & pop" bike shop. Family oriented, and friendly. Customers and homeless are both afforded respect. Many "custom" shops have come and gone in Oceanside, during the " Orange County Chopper" craze through the " "Sons of Anarchy" craze, Bill's shop crushed the competition with good quality used bikes, friendly advice, and excellent mechanic service, not to mention being a positive part of the community of Oceanside thru charity's and events.  They are the real deal, not a "chain store" of bikes.</Review>

Stopped by after a long week after gettng used to short weeks during the holidays. Ordered the bacon sandwich without the bacon, but rather than just stopping there the guy blew my mind by offering me some avocado and tomato on there. <Time>1504362709421</Time><Rating>3</Rating>< Review>
Passing by at 6:45 AM. Clients seem to be male, older or on their way to work. Noisy to order, but pleasant staff, though busy with drive through (only one parking space and that's for disabled), so you wait, and wait. There is only one person to make what you want. Beware, they put your cup inside another so its not too hot to hold, rather than give you a slip on, only trouble is that its difficult to get the plastic top off if you want to add cream or non fat milk, sugar etc.. A small is a medium in most places, and much the same price. In my opinion the coffee is nothing special to taste.<//Review>
